           <h1 class="entry-title">
            <a href="/blog/2018/7/11/las-vegas-elopement-photography-romy-david">
             Las Vegas Elopement Photography | Romy + David
            </a>
           </h1>
           <div class="entry-info">
            <span class="published">
             <a class="permalink" href="/blog/2018/7/11/las-vegas-elopement-photography-romy-david" title="Permalink">
              <time datetime="2018-07-12">

                <p>
                 I love these two so damn much!! Romy's short laced wedding dress is something I have never seen before and if you pay attention you'll notice her awesome Wifey4Lifey pocketbook.
                </p>
                <p>
                 They are freaking gorgeous, could do no wrong and the looks they throw are just plain HOT!
                </p>
                <p>

                </p>

          <header>
           <h1 class="entry-title">
            <a href="/blog/2018/6/12/estateonsecond">
             Estate On Second Wedding | Perla + Isai
            </a>
           </h1>
           <div class="entry-info">
            <span class="published">
             <a class="permalink" href="/blog/2018/6/12/estateonsecond" title="Permalink">
              <time datetime="2018-06-13">
               June 13, 2018
              </time>
             </a>
            </span>
            in
            <span class="category">
             <a href="/?category=weddings" rel="tag">
              weddings
             </a>
             ,
             <a href="/?category=wedding" rel="tag">
              wedding
             </a>
            </span>
           </div>
          </header>
          <!--POST BODY-->
          <div class="body entry-content">
           <div class="sqs-layout sqs-grid-12 columns-12" data-layout-label="Post Body" data-type="item" data-updated-on="1528863033454" id="item-5b2092401ae6cf43f6e02f4b">
            <div class="row sqs-row">
             <div class="col sqs-col-12 span-12">
              <div class="sqs-block html-block sqs-block-html" data-block-type="2" id="block-b0bbf05255111f004ce5">
               <div class="sqs-block-content">
                <p>
                 This Venue! I am officially in love with
                 <a href="http://estateonsecond.com" target="_blank">
                  The Estate on Second
                 </a>
                 in Santa Ana. It is to die for!!! And then couple it with the amazing work of
                 <a href="http://www.penelopepots.com" target="_blank">
                  Penelope Pots Floral Design
                 </a>
                 and Grounded Dream Events and it's un-freaking-believable.
                </p>
                <p>
                 Perla + Isai seriously killed it! So stunning and so much love and then topped it with a reception full of group games instead of dancing. It was definitely a wedding day I'll never forget.
                </p>
               </div>
              </div>

          <!--SPECIAL CONTENT-->
          <!--POST HEADER-->
          <header>
           <h1 class="entry-title">
            <a href="/blog/2018/5/1/intimate-san-diego-wedding-photographer-laura-aaron">
             Intimate San Diego Wedding Photographer | Laura + Aaron
            </a>
           </h1>
           <div class="entry-info">
            <span class="published">
             <a class="permalink" href="/blog/2018/5/1/intimate-san-diego-wedding-photographer-laura-aaron" title="Permalink">
              <time datetime="2018-05-02">
               May 02, 2018
              </time>
             </a>
            </span>
            in
            <span class="category">
             <a href="/?category=weddings" rel="tag">
              weddings
             </a>
            </span>
           </div>
          </header>
          <!--POST BODY-->
          <div class="body entry-content">
           <div class="sqs-layout sqs-grid-12 columns-12" data-layout-label="Post Body" data-type="item" data-updated-on="1525220540818" id="item-5ae900548a922d1389adaad1">
            <div class="row sqs-row">
             <div class="col sqs-col-12 span-12">
              <div class="sqs-block html-block sqs-block-html" data-block-type="2" id="block-yui_3_17_2_1_1525219292603_1480987">
               <div class="sqs-block-content">
                <p>
                 From our first FaceTime I could tell Laura + Aaron were a little quirky but super simple. They weren't looking for anything big, they didn't want to be the center of attention but images were crazy important to Laura. So these two opted for a tiny ceremony in an adorable chapel and a yummy dinner with all their favorite people.They nixed all the normal traditions and formalities but made extra time to run around the cliffs with us during sunset. (Our favorite!!)
                </p>
                <p>
                 Their day was dreamy, super chill and full of love!
                </p>
                <p>
                 Hair/Makeup -
                 <a href="http://twighair.com" target="_blank">
                  Twig Hair Lounge
                 </a>
                 <br/>
                 Gown -
                 <a href="https://www.bhldn.com" target="_blank">
                  BHLDN
                 </a>
                 <br/>
                 Florals -
                 <a href="http://www.pennyblooms.com" target="_blank">
                  Penny Blooms
                 </a>
                 <br/>
                 Ceremony -
                 <a href="http://ucsdlutheran.net" target="_blank">
                  University Lutheran Church
                 </a>
                 <br/>
                 Dinner Reception -
                 <a href="https://www.cataniasd.com" target="_blank">
                  Catania
                 </a>
                </p>
                <p>
                </p>
               </div>
